# Theorem Ledger

STATUS := machine-generated proof portfolio index

PURPOSE := list Lean theorem/lemma declarations as repository-local proof evidence, while separating proved local objects from unsupported frontier closure claims.

BOUNDARY := this ledger is an index, not a claim that every frontier program is solved.
BOUNDARY := this ledger does not prove P vs NP, Chronos-RR, gravity, cosmology, or foundations-of-physics closure.
BOUNDARY := entries inherit the exact scope of their Lean statements only.

VALIDATION_SURFACE :=
- `lake build` or targeted module builds remain the authority for Lean correctness.
- executable verifiers remain the authority for artifact/status-lock claims.
- CI status remains the authority for merged repository validation.

TOTAL_INDEXED_DECLARATIONS := 1629

## Allowed public claim

This repository contains a growing portfolio of Lean theorem and lemma declarations that can be inspected, built, and tied to verifier-backed boundary artifacts.

## Forbidden public claim

This ledger must not be used to claim solved open problems, unconditional physics closure, general proof efficiency, or theorem-complete closure beyond the exact Lean statements listed above.
